<Resp>None<//Resp>< Review>
No church/community can be fairly evaluated based on a single or isolated experience, which is why it took me almost a year of attending to share my impressions: Arcade, like other human-run churches, is not perfect; however, Pastor Craig is an experienced, highly qualified and bold leader who passionately teaches the Word with perspectives and interpretations relevant to current issues and events we deal with‚Äîbe they personal, political, et al. The church provides dedicated sessions/classrooms for kids and youth so they are not part of the adult sermons/congregation; however, it is up to the individual parent to utilize these resources.
Totally Worth Exploring

This church lacks the diversity of its locale; however, the leadership is actively engaged at outreach to address this‚Äîand I along with many others are overwhelmingly convinced of the leadership‚Äôs sincerity. I consider it a blessing to be a part of this community of believers and look forward to becoming a formal member. May their efforts continue to be blessed, their human imperfections and limited resources notwithstanding. If you are in the 95821 or in close proximity this church is worth exploring.< /Review>

< Text>
Groupon Buyers Beware! Apparently, my Honda Civic has four glass areas that are not considered to be part of the one large section of glass that makes up the four side windows. That section divides, according to Mike's Tint Shop, the windows into four more windows. The Groupon deal covers 5 windows only. But there is nothing in the fine print to examine your windows to see if you have more than 5 sections of glass. At the minimum you will have to pay an extra $51 in addition to whatever groupon package you purchased. VERY MISLEADING.

< Review>
Enjoyed our overnight stay here - we got to use the pool (by appointment only) and the room was well laid out. It's not a huge place so it's easy to walk the grounds and not get lost and you'll definitely want to because of all the cool topiary animals they have. Seriously talented landscaping - the kids loved it.

Probably could use better cleaning products - there was a sticky residue left on all high tough surfaces from whatever they used. We knew we would need to wipe everything down for peace of mind anyway so not a big deal.

Staff were nice, easy to find off the freeway, close to all sorts of dining choices (even though we only went to Habit Burger and Coldstones).

We'll probably stop at more Best Western Plus inns in the future because we enjoyed this one so much.<//Review>

<Text>Nice place to stay in Goleta and the greater Santa Barbara area.

When I stay at a hotel I have a few criteria that I often look at when I make a rating.

Is it in a safe location?
Yes, the area felt very safe. The hotel and it's parking lot felt very safe, well lighted. I had no concerns about my safety.

Is the hotel clean?
The hotel was very clean. Both the rooms and the grounds were clean and in good repair.  The bedding was tidy and clean, the floor was vacuumed, the bathrooms were spotless. On top of that the facility as a whole was very well cared for. The trash bins were emptied, the surfaces of the tables were not sticky and not dirty.

Are the staff friendly and pleasant?
We checked in with a very large group of over 50 high school boys, parents, coaches and the staff could have been overwhelmed, frustrated and rude but they were not. They were very pleasant to talk to, they took their time to inform us about the area and explain about the free breakfast, location of the rooms and more. It was a great experience.< /Text>< pictures>

< Review>
I stayed in room 104, the room was clean and well maintained and foot traffic outside was entirely reasonable. The breakfast was tasty and the range of options were nice, however it is only offered relatively early (until 9:30). I didn't use the pool, but it appeared clean and appealing.
I have two gripes: one, the wheelchair access and wheeled luggage access is off to the side with stairs cutting the lobby in half; two, while this is understandable it was quite irritating, there was construction going on in the adjacent room from 8am until 5pm which was extremely loud.
Overall the experience was quite good, allowing for the uncommon construction event.</Review>

< text>
We stayed at the Best Western Plus South Coast Inn on nights of May 8-10 in a room with 2 queen beds on the 2nd floor.  The room was spacious and clean, but the shower door leaked so that water came out of the shower stall onto the floor.  The breakfasts were good with an ample variety of breakfast foods.  The location was convenient, and the grounds were well kept and quite lovely.

Unfortunately, when we returned for another night on May 14, we were assigned a room on the 1st floor.  When we were turning in for the night, my husband discovered a huge bug crawling out of the pillow case.  It looked like a cockroach.  We notified the front desk, and were able to change to a room on the 2nd floor in another building.  This was a huge inconvenience considering we had to repack everything at midnight, plus a very unsettling experience, not knowing at which point bugs can crawl around in the bedding and in the room.

The next morning upon check-out, the staff apologized profusely, and gave us a $40 refund (50% of what we owed) for the room.  It's a shame that this should happen at such a reputable Inn, but I feel they need to be more vigilant about fumigation to control the bug problem.< /text>
